 [![Lando Calrissian and Chewbacca brought a citizens' fleet to Exegol to defeat the Sith Eternal forces.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/GalaxyFleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20200318010833) [![Lando Calrissian and Chewbacca brought a citizens' fleet to Exegol to defeat the Sith Eternal forces.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/GalaxyFleet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200318010833)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/GalaxyFleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20200318010833) 

Lando Calrissian and Chewbacca brought a citizens' fleet to Exegol to defeat the Sith Eternal forces.

 

Just then, Poe hears Lando's voice on the comlink, reassuring him that "there are more of them." Shortly later, Lando and Chewbacca arrive in the *Millennium Falcon*, accompanied by a massive [Citizens' Fleet](/wiki/Citizens%27_Fleet "Citizens' Fleet"), including Rebellion hero Commander [Wedge Antilles](/wiki/Wedge_Antilles "Wedge Antilles"), who compliments Lando's flying as he guns on the *Falcon*. The reinforcements reinvigorate the Resistance forces. Poe orders the combined forces to take out the Sith Star Destroyers' world-destroying superlaser cannons as it will save the galaxy. As several Sith Star Destroyers go up in flames, Pryde asks where they got these fighter craft since they have no navy. Admiral Griss replies that the armada is not a navy, but are just people. Poe is also relieved that his former associate Zorii Bliss has come to their aid.

Back at the Sith Citadel, the rejuvenated Emperor reveals himself to his Sith followers, who chant in unison. Ben rises to his feet but the Dark Lord levitates him in mid-air. Sidious tells Ben that he will be the last Skywalker and uses the Force to throw him into a nearby chasm, seemingly killing him. Determined to let nothing stop the return of the Sith, Sidious unleashes Force lightning on the Resistance fleet and allied armada, destroying several ships, including the *Tantive IV*, and killing Resistance members like [Lieutenant Commander](/wiki/Lieutenant_Commander "Lieutenant Commander") Nunb.

As Rey lies on the ground, she repeatedly says "be with me", continuing contacting the Jedi spirit and connecting to the pure cosmic energy of the entire universe. She then hears the voice of Luke and his father's Master [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") telling her that these are her final steps and telling her to rise and take them. This is followed by the voices of Luke's father Anakin Skywalker, Anakin's former apprentice [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"), and [Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") calling out her name. Anakin urges Rey to bring back the balance to the Force [as he did](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"). The voice of Master [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli") calls on Rey to find the light.

The voice of Master [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") reassures Rey that she has never been alone. The voice of Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") tells Rey that every Jedi who has ever lived lives in her. Anakin then reminds Rey that the Force surrounds her while Master [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura") tells Rey to let the Force guide her as Ahsoka's voice finishes the statement. Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") tells her to feel the Force while Anakin tells her to let it lift her. The voice of Master [Adi Gallia](/wiki/Adi_Gallia "Adi Gallia") encourage Rey to rise while Qui-Gon tells her that they stand behind her.

Obi-Wan calls out to Rey while Yoda urges Rey to rise. The voice of Kanan tells Rey that in the heart of a Jedi lies their strength. Obi-Wan then joins the other Jedi in urging Rey to rise, lending their strength to the weakened woman. As she rises to her feet, Luke tells her that the Force will be with her always. Drawing Leia's lightsaber, Rey confronts Sidious, who halts his attack on the fleet.

Believing that he is at the cusp of victory, the Sith Lord taunts Rey that her death will be the final word in the story of Rebellion. Sidious angrily attempts to kill Rey with Force lightning, but she deflects it back with Leia's lightsaber. Free of the Force lightning attack, Poe urges the allied fleet to make a final offensive against the Sith Star Destroyers, which have ascended into Exegol's upper atmosphere.

Continuing the Force lightning attack on Rey, the Sith Lord angrily taunts her that she is nothing more than a scavenger girl and no match for the power in him. Darth Sidious boasts that he is all the Sith, but Rey retorts that she is all the Jedi. Using the Force to retrieve Luke's lightsaber, she crosses blades and uses them to push back the Dark Lord's Force lightning attack. The Emperor is disintegrated by his own Force lightning, which triggers a massive wave of energy that destroys the throne of the Sith and the auditorium, crushing and killing all of his followers.

### Victory and Sacrifice[]

 [![Rey and Ben Solo acknowledge their connection and feelings for each other by sharing a kiss after Darth Sidious' demise.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/BenandReyKiss-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200329212013) [![Rey and Ben Solo acknowledge their connection and feelings for each other by sharing a kiss after Darth Sidious' demise.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/BenandReyKiss-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200329212013)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/BenandReyKiss-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200329212013) 

Rey and Ben Solo acknowledge their connection and feelings for each other by sharing a kiss after Darth Sidious' demise.

 

Meanwhile, on the *Steadfast*, Jannah connects the cables on a hijacked [laser cannon](/wiki/Laser_cannon "Laser cannon"), which opens fire on the bridge of the command ship. On the Resurgent Star Destroyer, Allegiant General Pryde watches in horror as the Resistance destroys the Sith fleet. Moments later he is killed when the bridge explodes. An [Abednedo](/wiki/Abednedo "Abednedo") pilot named [C'ai Threnalli](/wiki/C%27ai_Threnalli "C'ai Threnalli") tells Poe that the *Steadfast* has been destroyed. The Resistance and allied armada take out the remaining Sith forces.

Meanwhile, Finn and Jannah cling on to dear life as the stricken *Steadfast* descends into the atmosphere. Poe wants to rescue Finn and Jannah but Lando and Chewbacca use the *Falcon* to rescue the two Resistance fighters, who jump to safety before the *Steadfast* crashes onto the surface and disintegrates.

Back at the Sith Citadel, an exhausted Rey dies as a result of the duel with the Sith Lord. Her death is sensed through the Force by Finn. Shortly later, a hand appears at the edge of the chasm and an injured Ben pulls himself up, falling to his knees beside Rey and pulling her dead body into his lap. He embraces Rey's body. Pulling away, Ben puts his hand on her stomach and uses the [Force](/wiki/Force_healing "Force healing") to resurrect her. Rey awakens, smiling at Ben and touching his cheek gently. The two embrace before Rey kisses him. After they kiss, Ben smiles at her as he closes his eyes. Moments later, he falls backward and vanishes, having given his remaining life essence to Rey. His body fades away at the same moment that Leia's body becomes one with the Force. Maz Kanata also senses Ben's death from afar.

As the wrecked Sith fleet crashes on the surface of Exegol, Finn and Poe spot *Red Five*. Finn tells Poe that people are [rising up](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order") against the First Order all over the galaxy and the two say they did it. On [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"), a damaged Resurgent Star Destroyer descends into the atmosphere below [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City"). On [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"), the [Ewok](/wiki/Ewok "Ewok") war hero [Wicket W. Warrick](/wiki/Wicket_Wystri_Warrick "Wicket Wystri Warrick") and his son, [Pommet](/wiki/Pommet_Warrick "Pommet Warrick"), watch as another First Order Star Destroyer is destroyed by a [heavy freighter](/wiki/Unidentified_heavy_freighter "Unidentified heavy freighter") via the "Holdo manuever" in the skies above the moon. On [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), a stricken Resurgent Star Destroyer crashes, joining a [wrecked](/wiki/Inflictor "Inflictor") [Imperial Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial-class Star Destroyer") from the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku").

### Triumph of the Resistance[]

:   "*People are rising up all over the galaxy. Poe, we did it.*""*We did it.*"
:   ―Finn and Poe Dameron[[11]](#cite_note-IX-11)

 [![Uprisings against the First Order erupted across the galaxy, including Endor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Uprising_on_Endor.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315163407) [![Uprisings against the First Order erupted across the galaxy, including Endor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Uprising_on_Endor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200315163407)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Uprising_on_Endor.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315163407) 

Uprisings against the First Order erupted across the galaxy, including Endor.

 

The Resistance and the galaxy at large celebrate their victory against Sidious and the Sith Eternal. On Ajan Kloss, the victorious pilots and Resistance fighters embrace each other. Finn watches as Rose hugs Chewbacca. [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata") bestows Chewbacca with a [Medal of Bravery](/wiki/Medal_of_Bravery "Medal of Bravery"), which Han and Luke were awarded following the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"). Poe and Zorii exchange a look and it seems like Poe is trying to ask Zorii if she would like to celebrate with him privately, to which she shakes her head.

Poe then hugs Finn. Shortly later, Rey returns aboard *Red Five*. Jannah asks Lando where he is from and he tells her that he is from the [Gold system](/wiki/Gold_system "Gold system"). Lando in turn asks Jannah where she is from, and she tells him that she doesn't know, and Lando responds by saying "well, let's find out." Rey sees Finn and Poe, and the three of them embrace.

### Heir to the Skywalkers[]

:   "*I'm Rey.*""*Rey who?*""*Rey Skywalker.*"
:   ―Rey Skywalker and the Tatooine elder[[11]](#cite_note-IX-11)

 [![Rey adopts the Skywalker surname.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/ReySkywalker.png/revision/latest?cb=20200317091010) [![Rey adopts the Skywalker surname.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/ReySkywalker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200317091010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/ReySkywalker.png/revision/latest?cb=20200317091010) 

Rey adopts the Skywalker surname.

 

On [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"), Rey flies the *Millennium Falcon* past a [Jawa](/wiki/Jawa "Jawa") [sandcrawler](/wiki/Sandcrawler "Sandcrawler"). Together with BB-8, Rey visits the abandoned [Lars homestead](/wiki/Lars_homestead "Lars homestead"), where she buries Luke and Leia's lightsabers in the sand, having now built [her own](/wiki/Rey%27s_lightsaber "Rey's lightsaber")— a new black-handled lightsaber with a yellow blade. [A local](/wiki/Unidentified_Tatooine_elder "Unidentified Tatooine elder") asks her name and, seeing ghosts of Luke and Leia look on, Rey gives her name as "Rey Skywalker." Rey and BB-8 then watch the [twin suns](/wiki/Binary_star_system "Binary star system") of Tatooine rise.

## Development[]

### Writing[]

:   "*To have no script and to have a release date and have it be essentially a two-year window when you're saying (to yourself), you've got two years from the decision to do it to release, and you have literally nothing... You don't have the story, you don't have the cast, you don't have the designers, the sets. There was a crew, and there were things that will be worked on for the version that preceded ours, but this was starting over.*"
:   ―J.J. Abrams, on taking over from Colin Trevorrow[[12]](#cite_note-fast_company-12)

 [![J.J](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/JJ_Abrams.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130124230802) [![J.J](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/JJ_Abrams.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130124230802)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/JJ_Abrams.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130124230802) 

J.J. Abrams, director of *The Rise of Skywalker*

 
 [![Colin Trevorrow was originally designated as director for Episode IX.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/Colin_Trevorrow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150815192603) [![Colin Trevorrow was originally designated as director for Episode IX.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/Colin_Trevorrow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150815192603)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/Colin_Trevorrow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150815192603) 

Colin Trevorrow was originally designated as director for Episode IX.

 

Long before Lucasfilm's acquisition by Disney in [2012](/wiki/2012 "2012"), *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* creator [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") mentioned that he had plans to make nine films.[[13]](#cite_note-George's_Galactic_Empire-13) In [1976](/wiki/1976 "1976"), Lucas asked [Mark Hamill](/wiki/Mark_Hamill "Mark Hamill") to make a cameo in the film ("like [Obi-Wan](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") handing the lightsaber down to the next new hope"), which he estimated at the time would be filmed "around [2011](/wiki/2011 "2011")."[[14]](#cite_note-7,_8_&_9-14) According to Hamill, Lucas's outline for the sequel trilogy had [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") surviving until Episode IX and training [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") in the Force;[[15]](#cite_note-George's_Original_Ep._IX-15) Hamill was an advocate for this version of the story.[[16]](#cite_note-Hamill+Lucas'EpisodeIX-16) Producer [Gary Kurtz](/wiki/Gary_Kurtz "Gary Kurtz") mentioned in a [1999](/wiki/1999 "1999") interview that Lucas's plans for Episode IX included the first appearance of [the Emperor](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), a plot point ultimately used in the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy")'s [conclusion](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi").[[17]](#cite_note-TFN_Gary_Kurtz's_Interview-17)

Both [J.J. Abrams](/wiki/J.J._Abrams "J.J. Abrams") and [Rian Johnson](/wiki/Rian_Johnson "Rian Johnson") were rumored to be involved with early development for Episode IX,[[18]](#cite_note-18)[[19]](#cite_note-19) though they each denied this,[[20]](#cite_note-Future_of_Star_Wars-20)[[21]](#cite_note-JohnsonTwitter-21) with Abrams saying on his part, "We don't write a treatment but there are countless times we came up with something and said 'oh, this would be so great for Episode VIII!' or 'That's what we could get to in IX!'"[[20]](#cite_note-Future_of_Star_Wars-20) According to *The Force Awakens* co-writer [Lawrence Kasdan](/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan "Lawrence Kasdan"), the Lucasfilm creative team developed a general idea early on as to how they wanted the film to end.[[22]](#cite_note-Lucasfilm's_General_Idea-22) This was echoed by [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") actor [Adam Driver](/wiki/Adam_Driver "Adam Driver"): "With *Star Wars*, I had one piece of information of where it was all going, and that's where it has been in my head for a long time, and things were building towards that."[[23]](#cite_note-23)

In [August](/wiki/August "August") [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015"), [Colin Trevorrow](/wiki/Colin_Trevorrow "Colin Trevorrow") was announced as director for Episode IX.[[24]](#cite_note-Trevorrow_Confirmed-24) As Abrams and Johnson had to ensure a smooth transition between Episodes VII and VIII, Johnson and Trevorrow worked closely to ensure continuity between their respective films.[[25]](#cite_note-25) With cinematographer [John Schwartzman](/wiki/John_Schwartzman "John Schwartzman"), Trevorrow planned to shoot on [65 mm film](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/70_mm_film "wikipedia:70 mm film"), and wanted to capture some footage in actual [outer space](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Outer_space "wikipedia:Outer space").[[26]](#cite_note-65mm-26)[[27]](#cite_note-27) He contributed two spaceship designs for the movie—the [TIE Echelon](/wiki/TIE/es_assault_shuttle "TIE/es assault shuttle") and the TIE Marauder—the former of which was ultimately used for [*Star Wars*: Galaxy's Edge](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galaxy%27s_Edge "Star Wars: Galaxy's Edge").[[28]](#cite_note-28)[[29]](#cite_note-29) In early December of 2016,[[30]](#cite_note-30) following a collaboration with his frequent writing partner [Derek Connolly](/wiki/Derek_Connolly "Derek Connolly"), Trevorrow presented a completed script to Lucasfilm (as well as Lucas and Hamill)[[31]](#cite_note-Trevorrow-Empire-31)—entitled [*Duel of the Fates*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_Duel_of_the_Fates "Star Wars: Episode IX Duel of the Fates").[[32]](#cite_note-32)[[33]](#cite_note-33)

### Death of Carrie Fisher[]

:   "*The minute she finished, she grabbed me and said, 'I'd better be at the forefront of IX!' Because Harrison was front and center on VII, and Mark is front and center on VIII. She thought IX would be her movie. And it would have been.*"
:   ―Kathleen Kennedy, on Carrie Fisher's death[[34]](#cite_note-CarriesDeath-34)

 [![Carrie Fisher and co-star Mark Hamill in a promotional image for The Last Jedi](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f8/Skywalker_Twins_VF.png/revision/latest?cb=20170919045315) [![Carrie Fisher and co-star Mark Hamill in a promotional image for The Last Jedi](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f8/Skywalker_Twins_VF.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170919045315)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f8/Skywalker_Twins_VF.png/revision/latest?cb=20170919045315) 

Carrie Fisher and co-star Mark Hamill in a promotional image for *The Last Jedi*

 

[Carrie Fisher](/wiki/Carrie_Fisher "Carrie Fisher") died on [December 27](/wiki/December_27 "December 27"), 2016. Given that her character had featured prominently in Trevorrow's script,[[34]](#cite_note-CarriesDeath-34)[[35]](#cite_note-Original_Role_&_How_Much_Footage-35) the filmmaker met with Lucasfilm president [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") in [January](/wiki/January "January") [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017") to discuss possible story solutions.[[36]](#cite_note-Possible_Solutions-36) Kennedy said that the team had "pretty much started over,"[[37]](#cite_note-Process_Reboot-37) [Jack Thorne](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jack_Thorne "wikipedia:Jack Thorne") was briefly hired to rewrite the initial script,[[38]](#cite_note-Thorne_writing-38) but according to Thorne, "the process was tough and didn't end well."[[39]](#cite_note-Thorne_Guardian-39) In [September](/wiki/September "September") 2017, it was announced that Trevorrow had left the project due to creative differences,[[40]](#cite_note-Colin_Out-40) and that he would be replaced by Abrams.[[1]](#cite_note-JJ_Abrams-1) According to Kennedy, it was during the initial scripting phase that she realized Trevorrow wasn't the right person for the job;[[41]](#cite_note-NYT_Kennedy-41) she attributed this to Trevorrow having not been present at the story conferences for *The Force Awakens*, during which a basic plan for the trilogy had been laid out.[[42]](#cite_note-Gizmodo-Kennedy-42) (Trevorrow went on to direct and co-write [*Jurassic World: Dominion*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jurassic_World:_Dominion "wikipedia:Jurassic World: Dominion"), for which he viewed his *Episode IX* experience as a "practice run." Crewmembers from his *Episode IX* team joined him on the project.[[43]](#cite_note-Cancelled_SW_movie-43))

Disney reportedly agreed to pay a fee to [Paramount Pictures](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paramount_Pictures "wikipedia:Paramount Pictures") so that Abrams could make the film, as he had been in breach of contract with the latter by his involvement in *The Force Awakens*.[[44]](#cite_note-Paramount's_Payment-44) Abrams pitched his story to Disney head [Bob Iger](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bob_Iger "wikipedia:Bob Iger") in [December](/wiki/December "December") 2017[[45]](#cite_note-Story_Pitched-45) and had a script ready by [February](/wiki/February "February") [2018](/wiki/2018 "2018").[[46]](#cite_note-Abrams'_Script-46) As he told [*Rolling Stone*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rolling_Stone "wikipedia:Rolling Stone"), "I had no intention to return. But when the opportunity presented itself to finish a story that we had begun with these new characters, to tell the last chapter of their story, it felt like there was a chance to do it in a way where we could go beyond, and do better than we did in Seven."[[47]](#cite_note-47)

Due to the time constraints and pressure of returning to the series, Abrams asked [Chris Terrio](/wiki/Chris_Terrio "Chris Terrio") to co-write the film.[[12]](#cite_note-fast_company-12) In [May](/wiki/May "May") 2018, he told [*The Wall Street Journal*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal "wikipedia:The Wall Street Journal"): "I had a bunch of ideas from the beginning, back on VII, of where the story would go. I just never in my wildest dreams thought I would have a chance to execute them."[[48]](#cite_note-48) The creative team met with Lucas,[[49]](#cite_note-Lucas-49) Johnson, and Kasdan before writing the script;[[50]](#cite_note-GMA_Abrams-50) according to Abrams, Lucas explained many of his own ideas about [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") and the [midi-chlorians](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian").[[51]](#cite_note-George's_Ideas_:)-51) Terrio also spent some time doing extensive research into the [Expanded Universe](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") and [recent *Star Wars* animation](/wiki/Category:Canon_animated_television_series "Category:Canon animated television series");[[52]](#cite_note-52) he was influenced by many of those stories in writing the film, comparing the process to writing nonfiction: "When we would make a story decision, we were fully aware that this now will become canon, and so are we sure that this is the right story decision? Are we sure about it character-wise? Are we sure about it thematically? Does it seem like it gels with George's original intentions from Episode IV? Does it gel with what we learned in the prequels and what we learned in the sequel trilogy?"[[53]](#cite_note-RS-Terrio-53) He thought of the core characters as analogous to children of revolutionaries who fought in the [War of 1812](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/War_of_1812 "wikipedia:War of 1812").[[54]](#cite_note-54)

Abrams and Terrio were determined to make a film that would conclude the Skywalker saga and tie together the previous eight chapters.[[49]](#cite_note-Lucas-49)[[55]](#cite_note-55) The pair began the process by writing ideas on a series of dry erase boards at [Bad Robot](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bad_Robot "wikipedia:Bad Robot"), and then transferring them to a [Microsoft Word](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft_Word "wikipedia:Microsoft Word") document.[[56]](#cite_note-56) They would also meet in coffee shops to discuss the script, at which they would use code names to refer to the characters.[[57]](#cite_note-57) During the process, they collaborated on ideas with Kennedy, [Michelle Rejwan](/wiki/Michelle_Rejwan "Michelle Rejwan"), [Rick Carter](/wiki/Rick_Carter "Rick Carter"), [Roger Guyett](/wiki/Roger_Guyett "Roger Guyett"), [Kevin Jenkins](/wiki/Kevin_Jenkins "Kevin Jenkins"), [Michael Kaplan](/wiki/Michael_Kaplan "Michael Kaplan"), and [Neal Scanlan](/wiki/Neal_Scanlan "Neal Scanlan").[[53]](#cite_note-RS-Terrio-53) Kennedy and Rejwan gave them certain narrative beats that had to be hit.[[58]](#cite_note-58) Kennedy described the process to [Gizmodo](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gizmodo "wikipedia:Gizmodo"): "Nobody was being overly polite. If you didn't think something made sense. If you couldn't follow it, if you thought, from a fan's point of view, that you're stepping outside the lines and it was a bogus kind of thinking, no one was afraid to say that because we knew how important this was to get right. And we didn't let things go."[[42]](#cite_note-Gizmodo-Kennedy-42) Abrams also described it as "this crazy challenge that could have been a wildly uncomfortable contortion of ideas and shoving in of answers and Band-Aids and bridges … I feel like we've gotten to a place–without jinxing anything–where we might have something incredibly special."[[12]](#cite_note-fast_company-12) Terrio is quoted in *[The Art of Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker](/wiki/The_Art_of_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "The Art of Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker")* as saying "I've never rewritten a film as much as this one. It's like a tide. There's a new script every morning. But we just keep going at it and going at it, loosely thinking that it's not good enough. It's never good enough."[[59]](#cite_note-59)

The writers revisited some of the ideas Abrams and Kasdan had for *The Force Awakens*,[[60]](#cite_note-60) and also used some ideas that were present in Trevorrow's script.[[31]](#cite_note-Trevorrow-Empire-31) Some major elements of the plot originated in a 2014 Lucasfilm story meeting: Leia being involved in bringing her son back to the light, the notion of Leia being a mentor to Rey, and Rey being a metaphorical Skywalker.[[61]](#cite_note-ArtofROS-61) Certain aspects of the story changed significantly during pre-production,[[62]](#cite_note-Syfy-story-62) and the film had frequent dialogue changes from day to day.[[63]](#cite_note-63)[[41]](#cite_note-NYT_Kennedy-41) According to [Pablo Hidalgo](/wiki/Pablo_Hidalgo "Pablo Hidalgo"), Lucas and [Michael Arndt](/wiki/Michael_Arndt "Michael Arndt")'s original plan was that Episode IX's villain would come out of hiding on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant").[[64]](#cite_note-HidalgoCoruscant3rdact-64) Producer [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") claimed that Palpatine's return (an idea first used in *[Star Wars: Dark Empire](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Dark_Empire "Star Wars: Dark Empire")*) was planned from the beginning,[[65]](#cite_note-65) although Trevorrow believed it was a new idea by Abrams.[[31]](#cite_note-Trevorrow-Empire-31) According to Terrio, he and Abrams didn't use anything from Trevorrow's script, although "There may have been certain elements that we used that had been in the original script and we weren't aware of it. The Guild makes the determination about those things."[[66]](#cite_note-66) Regardless, Trevorrow and Connolly received story credits in the final film.[[4]](#cite_note-WGA-4) In regards to *The Last Jedi*'s influence on the film, Abrams told *[Esquire](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Esquire_(magazine) "wikipedia:Esquire (magazine)")*: "As a filmmaker, working on episode IX, amazingly, nothing that he [Rian Johnson] did in *Last Jedi* got in the way of things that we had talked about wanting to do down the line, ideas that I had about where things might go, so… it wasn't like his story somehow derailed the things I wanted to pursue. In fact, strangely, they might have even helped strengthen them because we got to make some choices that sort of take advantage of the fact that Rian hadn't done the things that we were thinking about doing."[[67]](#cite_note-67)

Lucasfilm dispelled rumors that it would digitally recreate Fisher in future films.[[68]](#cite_note-SW-A_Statement_Regarding_New_Rumors-68) Fisher's brother [Todd](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Todd_Fisher "wikipedia:Todd Fisher") said that he and [Billie Lourd](/wiki/Billie_Lourd "Billie Lourd") had granted Lucasfilm rights to use footage of her.[[69]](#cite_note-Carrie_in_Episode_IX-69) Kennedy initially claimed that Ms. Fisher would not appear in the film,[[70]](#cite_note-70) though Abrams later confirmed that Ms. Fisher would appear in the film via unused footage from *The Force Awakens*.[[5]](#cite_note-Cast_Announced-5) Mr. Fisher credited this decision to Abrams,[[71]](#cite_note-Eddie's_Thoughts-71) who said, "It was like finding this impossible answer to this impossible question."[[72]](#cite_note-72) According to Mr. Fisher: "There's a lot of minutes of footage. I don't mean just outtakes. This is unused, new content that could be woven into the storyline. That's what's going to give everybody such a great kick. It's going to look like it was meant to be. Like it was shot yesterday."[[73]](#cite_note-73) He also claimed that unused footage from *The Last Jedi* would also be used,[[74]](#cite_note-74) but Abrams later clarified that no footage from that film was used due to nothing substantial being available.[[75]](#cite_note-75) Ultimately, [ILM](/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic "Industrial Light & Magic") placed Fisher's facial performance onto a digital body, with an on-set stand-in serving as a visual reference for the actors. This allowed the character to be placed in new locations, and for the effects artists to give her different clothes and a new hairstyle that would be unique to *The Rise of Skywalker*.[[76]](#cite_note-76)

### Production[]

:   "*We went into this movie very much in the mindset that this has to be conclusive. It has to. You have to get some answers. You have to learn some things.*"
:   ―J.J. Abrams[[77]](#cite_note-FinnOrigin-77)

 [![Daisy Ridley, John Boyega, and Oscar Isaac on the set of the film, having completed filming](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Episode_IX_Wrap.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190215231112) [![Daisy Ridley, John Boyega, and Oscar Isaac on the set of the film, having completed filming](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Episode_IX_Wrap.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190215231112)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Episode_IX_Wrap.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190215231112) 

Daisy Ridley, John Boyega, and Oscar Isaac on the set of the film, having completed filming

 

Principal photography began at [Pinewood Studios](/wiki/Pinewood_Studios "Pinewood Studios") on [August 1](/wiki/August_1 "August 1"), [2018](/wiki/2018 "2018"),[[5]](#cite_note-Cast_Announced-5)[[78]](#cite_note-First_Day_Of_Filming-78) under the working title of "trlXie" (originally "Black Diamond").[[79]](#cite_note-New_Working_Title-79)[[80]](#cite_note-80) Production also took place in [Wadi Rum](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wadi_Rum "wikipedia:Wadi Rum"), [Jordan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jordan "wikipedia:Jordan") (the same filming location for [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha") in *[Rogue One: A Star Wars Story](/wiki/Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story "Rogue One: A Star Wars Story")*) for three weeks.[[81]](#cite_note-81) Some sequences were filmed with 65mm film and [IMAX](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IMAX "wikipedia:IMAX") cameras.[[82]](#cite_note-82)[[83]](#cite_note-83) Because the film was under a shortened production timeline, the crew had to shoot everything they needed during principal photography,[[84]](#cite_note-StarWarsShow-J.J._Abrams_&_Kelly_Marie_Tran_At_SWCC_2019_|_The_Star_Wars_Show_Live!-84) and [Maryann Brandon](/wiki/Maryann_Brandon "Maryann Brandon") began editing on set.[[85]](#cite_note-85) [Matt Smith](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matt_Smith "wikipedia:Matt Smith") was initially set to play a role in the film,[[86]](#cite_note-Smith_Confirmed-86) but by early 2019 the actor was no longer involved;[[87]](#cite_note-Smith_Interview-87) When he later spoke to the Happy Sad Confused podcast, Smith described his character as "a really groovy part and concept. It was a big thing, it was a big story detail, a transformative 'Star Wars' story detail and it never got quite over the line."[[88]](#cite_note-Smith_Ignites-88)

Abrams felt less creatively constrained in making *The Rise of Skywalker* than he did with *The Force Awakens*,[[89]](#cite_note-Vanity_Fair_Preview-89) citing Rian Johnson's work on *The Last Jedi* as the inspiration:[[90]](#cite_note-90) "Rian helped remind me that that's why we're on these movies—not to just do something that you've seen before."[[91]](#cite_note-91) According to [Poe Dameron](/wiki/Poe_Dameron "Poe Dameron") actor [Oscar Isaac](/wiki/Oscar_Isaac "Oscar Isaac"), the shooting of *The Rise of Skywalker* allowed for more improvisation than *The Force Awakens* or *The Last Jedi*: "It's a testament to J.J. coming back and feeling confident. There's less pressure for it to be right. We just want to make a good movie and have a really good time while doing it."[[92]](#cite_note-92) Abrams shot many of the character interactions in long takes, with actors sometimes coming up with their own lines.[[93]](#cite_note-93) [Daisy Ridley](/wiki/Daisy_Ridley "Daisy Ridley") also commented: "There was this thing: JJ would ask us to do the scene without speaking, just to feel the emotional… whatever. He was like, 'You never know what could come up.' We did that a couple of times. Then it became a joke, because we would just wet ourselves laughing."[[94]](#cite_note-94)

Prior to shooting, members of the cast were trained in various specialties to prepare for the shoot, such as kickboxing,[[95]](#cite_note-EWJJNOV19-95) horseback riding, using a bow-and-arrow and holding a gun.[[96]](#cite_note-96)[[97]](#cite_note-97) Ridley performed the majority of her character's stunts herself.[[98]](#cite_note-Ridley_stunts-98) Filmmaker [Kevin Smith](/wiki/Kevin_Smith "Kevin Smith") visited the set (just as he did for *The Force Awakens*) and described what he saw: "Biggest set I've ever seen in my life. The dude's not directing a movie, it's like he's directing a small country."[[99]](#cite_note-99) The script was under even greater security than those of previous films, with actors not allowed to take copies home;[[100]](#cite_note-100)[[101]](#cite_note-spoiler_security-101)[[102]](#cite_note-102) despite this, a copy was put up for sale on [eBay](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/eBay "wikipedia:eBay"), after [Finn](/wiki/Finn "Finn") actor [John Boyega](/wiki/John_Boyega "John Boyega") accidentally left it under his bed and it was found by a cleaning person. However, Lucasfilm was warned about it and recovered the script before someone could buy it.[[103]](#cite_note-Abrams_GMA-103)[[104]](#cite_note-New_York_Post_Script-104) By [December 11](/wiki/December_11 "December 11"), 2018, Hamill had worked for "about a week" on the film, but had yet to shoot most of his scenes, which he expected to do alongside his work on the TV series *[Knightfall](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knightfall_(TV_series) "wikipedia:Knightfall (TV series)")*.[[101]](#cite_note-spoiler_security-101)

Filming wrapped on [February 15](/wiki/February_15 "February 15"), [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019").[[105]](#cite_note-Wrapping_Day_Of_Filming-105) Reshoots reportedly took place between late September and mid-[October](/wiki/October "October") at [Bad Robot Productions](/wiki/Bad_Robot_Productions "Bad Robot Productions").[[106]](#cite_note-106)

### Post-production[]

[John Williams](/wiki/John_Williams "John Williams") had begun work on the [musical score](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_(soundtrack) "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker (soundtrack)") by May 2019,[[107]](#cite_note-107) and was scheduled to begin recording in June.[[108]](#cite_note-108) Recording took a total of 11 days from July through November of 2019.[[109]](#cite_note-109) Williams said that it will most likely be his final *Star Wars* project.[[7]](#cite_note-Williams_Done-7)

The film was the first project for a new ILM division in [Sydney, Australia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sydney "wikipedia:Sydney").[[110]](#cite_note-110) The Luke/Leia flashback scene was created by using the facial likenesses of the characters from *The Empire Strikes back* and *Return of the Jedi*, with Billie Lourd acting as a stand-in for Leia.[[111]](#cite_note-111) Abrams told *Entertainment Weekly* that the film had significantly less post-production time than normal, and that it was "literally a practical race to get it finished." However, he felt more confident about *The Rise of Skywalker* than he had *The Force Awakens*.[[95]](#cite_note-EWJJNOV19-95) The editing of *The Rise of Skywalker* was finished on [November 24](/wiki/November_24 "November 24"), [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019").[[112]](#cite_note-112) Taken as a whole, Abrams described the film as "the most challenging" project he'd ever been involved with.[[113]](#cite_note-113)[[114]](#cite_note-JJ-RS-114)

## Release and reception[]

### Reveals and release[]

:   "*The beauty of working with Chris Terrio and producing with Kathleen Kennedy is that I think we have found a way — I hope, it's up for you to decide — to bring this story to a conclusion in a way that feels satisfying, surprising, amusing, shocking, all the ways that a story should make you feel.*"
:   ―J.J. Abrams[[115]](#cite_note-Disneydecademovies-115)

The film was originally scheduled for release on [May 24](/wiki/May_24 "May 24"), [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019"),[[116]](#cite_note-May_24-116) but was later pushed back to [December 20](/wiki/December_20 "December 20"),[[8]](#cite_note-Jedi_Redeemed-8) giving the May 24 date to the [live-action remake](https://disney.fandom.com/wiki/Aladdin_(2019_film) "w:c:disney:Aladdin (2019 film)") of [*Aladdin*](https://disney.fandom.com/wiki/Aladdin_(1992_film) "w:c:disney:Aladdin (1992 film)").[[117]](#cite_note-Aladdin-117) Footage was first publicly screened at Disney's [March 8](/wiki/March_8 "March 8") investor's conference,[[118]](#cite_note-Investor_footage-118) and briefly at CinemaCon 2019 as part of a montage of upcoming Disney films.[[119]](#cite_note-119) The film was featured in a panel at [Celebration Chicago](/wiki/Celebration_Chicago "Celebration Chicago"), featuring director/co-writer J.J. Abrams and producer Kathleen Kennedy.[[120]](#cite_note-SW-Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_Panel_Coming_to_Star_Wars_Celebration_Chicago-120) The teaser trailer debuted at this event,[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX_panel-121) which also revealed the film's title and teaser poster.[[122]](#cite_note-SW-SWCC_2019:_13_Things_We_Learned_from_the_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Panel-122) During the convention, Abrams, Kennedy, and members of the cast were interviewed for [*Good Morning America*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Good_Morning_America "wikipedia:Good Morning America").[[50]](#cite_note-GMA_Abrams-50)[[123]](#cite_note-123) The film was featured in the May issue of *[Vanity Fair](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vanity_Fair "wikipedia:Vanity Fair")*,[[89]](#cite_note-Vanity_Fair_Preview-89) the November issues of [*Empire*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Empire_(film_magazine) "wikipedia:Empire (film magazine)"),[[124]](#cite_note-124) [*Entertainment Weekly*](/wiki/Entertainment_Weekly_Books "Entertainment Weekly Books") and [*Rolling Stone*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rolling_Stone "wikipedia:Rolling Stone"),[[95]](#cite_note-EWJJNOV19-95)[[125]](#cite_note-125)[[114]](#cite_note-JJ-RS-114) the December issue of [*People*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/People_(magazine) "wikipedia:People (magazine)"),[[126]](#cite_note-126) and the [January](/wiki/January "January") [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020") issue of *Empire*.[[127]](#cite_note-127) A panel was held at the 2019 [D23 Expo](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D23_(Disney) "wikipedia:D23 (Disney)"), featuring cast and crew, with the reveal of a new teaser poster and two show casings of footage;[[128]](#cite_note-128)[[129]](#cite_note-SW-D23_Expo_2019:_New_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Footage_and_More_Highlights_from_the_Walt_Disney_Studios_Panel-129) The latter of the two was later released online and aired on television.[[130]](#cite_note-130)

The cast and crew made a number of television appearances to promote the film, including *Good Morning America*,[[103]](#cite_note-Abrams_GMA-103)[[131]](#cite_note-131)[[132]](#cite_note-132)[[133]](#cite_note-133)[[134]](#cite_note-134) [*The Late Show With Stephen Colbert*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Late_Show_With_Stephen_Colbert "wikipedia:The Late Show With Stephen Colbert"),[[135]](#cite_note-135) [*The Tonight Show Starring Jimmy Fallon*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tonight_Show_Starring_Jimmy_Fallon "wikipedia:The Tonight Show Starring Jimmy Fallon"),[[136]](#cite_note-136)[[137]](#cite_note-137) [*Live with Kelly and Ryan*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Live_with_Kelly_and_Ryan "wikipedia:Live with Kelly and Ryan"),[[138]](#cite_note-138)[[139]](#cite_note-139) [*Late Night with Seth Meyers*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Night_with_Seth_Meyers "wikipedia:Late Night with Seth Meyers"),[[140]](#cite_note-140) and [*Jimmy Kimmel Live!*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jimmy_Kimmel_Live! "wikipedia:Jimmy Kimmel Live!").[[141]](#cite_note-141) The cast and crew participated in a livestream Q&A on [December 2](/wiki/December_2 "December 2"),[[142]](#cite_note-142) a press conference on [December 4](/wiki/December_4 "December 4").[[143]](#cite_note-143)[[144]](#cite_note-144) Brazil's [Comic Con Experience](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comic_Con_Experience "wikipedia:Comic Con Experience") on [December 7](/wiki/December_7 "December 7"),[[145]](#cite_note-145) and the film's Japan premiere on [December 11](/wiki/December_11 "December 11").[[146]](#cite_note-146) On [December 12](/wiki/December_12 "December 12"), Amazon.com released an exclusive behind-the-scenes video.[[147]](#cite_note-147) Tickets went on sale [October 21](/wiki/October_21 "October 21"),[[148]](#cite_note-148) followed by the release of the final trailer on [*Monday Night Football*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monday_Night_Football "wikipedia:Monday Night Football") and the theatrical poster.[[149]](#cite_note-149)[[150]](#cite_note-SW-See_the_Official_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Theatrical_Poster-150) Lucasfilm collaborated with [Porsche](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Porsche "wikipedia:Porsche") on a new *Star Wars* spaceship design that was built for the film's premiere,[[151]](#cite_note-151) named the [Tri-Wing S-91x Pegasus Starfighter](/wiki/Tri-Wing_S-91x_Pegasus_Starfighter "Tri-Wing S-91x Pegasus Starfighter").[[152]](#cite_note-152) Beginning on [December 18](/wiki/December_18 "December 18"), [AMC Theaters](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/AMC_Theaters "wikipedia:AMC Theaters") held a 27+ hour marathon of Episodes I through VIII, leading up to Episode IX.[[153]](#cite_note-153) Adam Driver, Greg Grunberg and Mark Hamill each held [Omaze](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Omaze "wikipedia:Omaze") fundraisers for which winners could attend the film's U.S. premiere,[[154]](#cite_note-154)[[155]](#cite_note-155)[[156]](#cite_note-156) which was held on [December 16](/wiki/December_16 "December 16").[[157]](#cite_note-SW-Watch_the_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Red_Carpet_Live_at_StarWars.com-157) As happened with *The Force Awakens*,[[158]](#cite_note-158) a dying fan was given a screening of the film, with Bob Iger himself confirming it on Twitter.[[159]](#cite_note-159)

### Box office and awards[]

*The Rise of Skywalker* opened to $177 million domestic and $376 million worldwide box office.[[160]](#cite_note-BOM-OW-160) Notably, it performed poorly in China, continuing a downward trend from *The Force Awakens*.[[161]](#cite_note-THR-China-161) The film went on to make over $1.074 billion worldwide.[[162]](#cite_note-BOM-total-162) The film has proven to be divisive amongst the *Star Wars* fanbase. Ridley has stated she is upset by this reputation because she does not want fans to feel like they walked away with something they do not like.[[163]](#cite_note-Jan29Josh-163)

*The Rise of Skywalker* received three nominations at the [92nd Academy Awards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/92nd_Academy_Awards "wikipedia:92nd Academy Awards"): [Best Original Score](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Original_Score "wikipedia:Academy Award for Best Original Score"), [Best Sound Editing](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Sound_Editing "wikipedia:Academy Award for Best Sound Editing"), and [Best Visual Effects](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Visual_Effects "wikipedia:Academy Award for Best Visual Effects").[[164]](#cite_note-HollywoodReporter-Oscars-164)

## Continuity[]

In the *[LEGO Star Wars: Droid Tales](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_Droid_Tales "LEGO Star Wars: Droid Tales")* episode "[Exit from Endor](/wiki/Exit_from_Endor "Exit from Endor")," [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2") has a backup of [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO")'s memories, which causes his eyes to glow when installed.[[165]](#cite_note-Exit_from_Endor-165) The film claims via Kylo Ren that Rey's parents "sold [her] to protect her," but this was recontextualized by the novel *[Shadow of the Sith](/wiki/Shadow_of_the_Sith "Shadow of the Sith")*,[[166]](#cite_note-Paid_with_Songsteel-166) which actually depicted the events surrounding Rey's final days with her parents, who were identified as [Dathan](/wiki/Dathan "Dathan") and [Miramir](/wiki/Miramir "Miramir").[[167]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-167) Instead of selling her, Dathan and Miramir actually paid [Unkar Plutt](/wiki/Unkar_Plutt "Unkar Plutt") with a [songsteel](/wiki/Songsteel "Songsteel") [charm](/wiki/Sith_Eternal_crest "Sith Eternal crest") to keep Rey hidden on Jakku.[[166]](#cite_note-Paid_with_Songsteel-166)

## Adaptations and tie-in media[]

In November 2018, Lucasfilm debuted the animated shorts *[Star Wars Galaxy of Adventures](/wiki/Star_Wars_Galaxy_of_Adventures "Star Wars Galaxy of Adventures")* as an introduction to the saga for children, beginning a year-long lead-up to the film.[[168]](#cite_note-Galaxy_of_Adventures-168) In December 2018, [Topps](/wiki/Topps "Topps") began a year-long campaign, dubbed "Star Wars Galactic Moments: Countdown to Episode IX," in which three cards were released each week leading up to the release of the film.[[169]](#cite_note-169) [Sith trooper](/wiki/Sith_trooper "Sith trooper") merchandise debuted in stores on [September 1](/wiki/September_1 "September 1"), 2019,[[170]](#cite_note-SW-Updated_-_The_Sith_Trooper_from_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Marches_to_Shelves-170) while the film's main merchandise push began on [October 4](/wiki/October_4 "October 4"), 2019, known as [Triple Force Friday](/wiki/Force_Friday "Force Friday"). Aside from *The Rise of Skywalker*, the event debuted merchandise for the TV series *[Star Wars: The Mandalorian](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Mandalorian "Star Wars: The Mandalorian")* and the video game *[Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order](/wiki/Star_Wars_Jedi:_Fallen_Order "Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order")*.[[171]](#cite_note-Triple_Force_Friday-171)

Lucasfilm partnered with eight product brands to promote the film: [Bose](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bose_Corporation "wikipedia:Bose Corporation"), [Dannon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danone "wikipedia:Danone"), [General Electric](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_Electric "wikipedia:General Electric"), [General Mills](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_Mills "wikipedia:General Mills"), [Porsche](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Porsche "wikipedia:Porsche"), [Samsung](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samsung "wikipedia:Samsung"), [McDonald's](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/McDonald%27s "wikipedia:McDonald's"), and [United Airlines](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Airlines "wikipedia:United Airlines")[[172]](#cite_note-Partners-172)—with each ad campaign beginning on [November 1](/wiki/November_1 "November 1").[[173]](#cite_note-173) Like with [*The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Journey_to_Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens "Journey to Star Wars: The Force Awakens") and [*The Last Jedi*](/wiki/Journey_to_Star_Wars:_The_Last_Jedi "Journey to Star Wars: The Last Jedi"), the months leading up to the debut of *The Rise of Skywalker* saw the release of tie-in novels, short stories, comics, reference books, and activity books known collectively as [Journey to *Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Journey_to_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Journey to Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker"). (Additional books would be released throughout 2020, including the [novel](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_Expanded_Edition "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: Expanded Edition"), [junior novel](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_A_Junior_Novel "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: A Junior Novel"), and [graphic novel](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Graphic_Novel_Adaptation "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker Graphic Novel Adaptation") adaptations of the film and the *Art of* book. The )[[174]](#cite_note-Journey_to_TROS-174) A comic adaptation from [Marvel Comics](/wiki/Marvel_Comics "Marvel Comics") was planned but ultimately canceled.[[175]](#cite_note-Comic_cancelation-175) *[Star Tours: The Adventures Continue](/wiki/Star_Tours:_The_Adventures_Continue "Star Tours: The Adventures Continue")* introduced *The Rise of Skywalker*–themed content.[[176]](#cite_note-SW-Star_Tours_to_Receive_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Update_on_December_20-176) [Funko](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Funko "wikipedia:Funko") released an animated short inspired by the film.[[177]](#cite_note-177)[[176]](#cite_note-SW-Star_Tours_to_Receive_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Update_on_December_20-176) Lucasfilm hosted *Star Wars* Nights at NBA games in December 2019 and January 2020.[[178]](#cite_note-SW-Star_Wars_Nights_Coming_to_Basketball_Arenas_in_Our_Galaxy-178)

Several Disney-owned video games were updated with content from the film: *[Disney Emoji Blitz](/wiki/Disney_Emoji_Blitz "Disney Emoji Blitz")*, *[Disney Magic Kingdoms](https://www.gameloft.com/en/game/disney-magic-kingdom)*, *[Star Wars: Commander](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Commander "Star Wars: Commander")*, *[Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galaxy_of_Heroes "Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes")*,[[179]](#cite_note-SW-New_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Updates_Coming_to_Mobile_Games-179) and *[Star Wars Battlefront II](/wiki/Star_Wars_Battlefront_II "Star Wars Battlefront II")*.[[180]](#cite_note-EA-Community_Transmission_–_A_look_ahead_at_what's_coming_in_2019-180) Beginning on December 12, *[Fortnite](/wiki/Fortnite "Fortnite")* rolled out a series of *The Rise of Skywalker* skins and emotes,[[181]](#cite_note-181) and on [December 14](/wiki/December_14 "December 14") previewed a scene from the film in an [in-game event](/wiki/Fortnite_X_Star_Wars "Fortnite X Star Wars").[[182]](#cite_note-182)[[183]](#cite_note-183) (The event concluded with exclusive Palpatine dialogue that has been interpreted as the transmission mentioned in the film's [opening crawl](/wiki/Opening_crawl "Opening crawl").[[184]](#cite_note-184)) [Roblox](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roblox "wikipedia:Roblox") also featured tie-in elements with the film.[[185]](#cite_note-SW-Star_Wars_and_Roblox_Join_Forces_for_the_Galactic_Speedway_Creator_Challenge-185) The video game *[LEGO Star Wars: The Skywalker Saga](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Skywalker_Saga "LEGO Star Wars: The Skywalker Saga")* will include levels from the film.

### Home video[]

While schedule for release on [March 17](/wiki/March_17 "March 17"), the film became available on most digital platforms in HD and 4K Ultra HD on [March 13](/wiki/March_13 "March 13").[[186]](#cite_note-186) A number of physical releases followed on [March 31](/wiki/March_31 "March 31"), including a Multiscreen Edition (Blu Ray and Digital Code), an Ultimate Collector's Edition (4K, Blu Ray, and Digital Code) and a DVD edition; [Best Buy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Best_Buy "wikipedia:Best Buy"), [Target](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Target_Corporation "wikipedia:Target Corporation"), and [Wal Mart](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wal_Mart "wikipedia:Wal Mart") will offer exclusive versions of the sets, as well as a 27-disc "Skywalker Saga" set (4K, Blu Ray, Digital Code) exclusive to Best Buy.[[187]](#cite_note-SW-The_End_of_the_Skywalker_Saga,_Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker,_Comes_Home-187)

Special features include:

* [The Skywalker Legacy](/wiki/The_Skywalker_Legacy "The Skywalker Legacy") – The story lives forever in this feature-length documentary that charts the making of *Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker*.
* Pasaana Pursuit: Creating the Speeder Chase – Dive into the making of the movie's epic landspeeder chase and discover how this spectacular sequence was brought to the screen.
* Aliens in the Desert – See what it took to create the Pasaana desert scenes, from the sheer scale and complexity of the shoot to its colorful details.
* D-O: Key to the Past – Explore the ship that connects Rey to the mystery of her missing parents and get to know the galaxy's newest, irresistible droid.
* Warwick & Son – Warwick Davis, who played Wicket in *Star Wars: Return of the Jedi*, dons the Ewok costume once more; this time joined by his son Harrison.
* Cast of Creatures – The team behind the film's memorable creatures reveal the puppetry, makeup, prosthetics and digital magic that bring them to life!
* The Maestro's Finale – Composer John Williams reflects on his body of work for the Star Wars saga and shares insights on scoring *Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker* (Digital Exclusive).

The Target exclusive edition features *[A Final Alliance](/wiki/A_Final_Alliance "A Final Alliance")* bonus featurette 25 minutes in length focusing on the ships and effects of the film.

The film was released on [Disney+](/wiki/Disney%2B "Disney+") on [May 4](/wiki/May_4 "May 4"), 2020—two months earlier than originally planned.[[188]](#cite_note-SW-Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker_Coming_to_Disney+_on_May_the_4th-188)

[189.441](#cite_ref-IX-Credits_189-441) [189.442](#cite_ref-IX-Credits_189-442) [189.443](#cite_ref-IX-Credits_189-443) ***Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*** Credits 190. ↑ [190.0](#cite_ref-CinemaBlend_190-0) [190.1](#cite_ref-CinemaBlend_190-1) [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) [Why Mark Hamill Got To Play With A Giant BB-8 In The Making Of Star Wars: The Last Jedi](https://www.cinemablend.com/news/2393012/why-mark-hamill-got-to-play-with-a-giant-bb-8-in-the-making-of-star-wars-the-last-jedi) by Eisenberg, Eric on [www.cinemablend.com](https://www.cinemablend.com) ([2018](/wiki/2018 "2018")): "I was very surprised that Rian [Johnson] billed me as Dobbu Scay… I thought it was going to be an Easter egg. I didn't say, 'Oh, I need billing.' And if I did have billing, in the past as a pseudonym I've used a combination of my brothers' names, and I call myself Patrick Williams." ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20200220161041/https://www.cinemablend.com/news/2393012/why-mark-hamill-got-to-play-with-a-giant-bb-8-in-the-making-of-star-wars-the-last-jedi) archived on [February 20](/wiki/February_20 "February 20"), [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020")) 191. [↑](#cite_ref-SpyUrban_191-0) [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) [The Boys and Star Trek star reveals secret Rise of Skywalker cameo](https://www.digitalspy.com/movies/a33444596/karl-urban-star-wars-rise-of-skywalker-cameo) by Susannah Alexander and Adam Tanswell on [www.digitalspy.com](https://www.digitalspy.com) ([July 18](/wiki/July_18 "July 18"), [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020")): "Confirming that the Karl Urban listed in the 'additional voices' section of the end credits of the 2019 film is indeed him, the actor explained how his cameo came about. "Here's the process," he said. "I had the good fortune to go and visit JJ Abrams [the film's director] while he was shooting *The Rise of Skywalker*. While I was there, he put me in a stormtrooper uniform and we had a really fun day on set. "It's been one of my life-long goals to be a stormtrooper, so I can tick that off now." He also pinpointed the moment in which he is seen (or rather, his stormtrooper costume is) and heard, which is during a scene set on Kylo Ren's (Adam Driver) spaceship. "What is in the cut is my voice saying 'Knights of Ren' as Kylo Ren walks down a hallway past two stormtroopers. I am one of those stormtroopers," he said." ([backup link](https://archive.is/ajaFH)) 192. [↑](#cite_ref-LandoVoice_192-0) [Instagram-Logo](https://instagram.com) Reggie Watts ([@reggiewatts](https://instagram.com/reggiewatts)) on [Instagram](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Instagram "wikipedia:Instagram") ([post](https://instagram.com/p/B7NwZZLhIDo) on [January 12](/wiki/January_12 "January 12"), [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020")): "I does voice of Lando in mask." ([screenshot](/wiki/File:ReggieWatts-LandoVoice-January-12-2020.png "File:ReggieWatts-LandoVoice-January-12-2020.png")) 193. [↑](#cite_ref-195) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) [Samantha Alleyne](/wiki/Samantha_Alleyne "Samantha Alleyne") ([@samkkalleyne](https://twitter.com/samkkalleyne)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/samkkalleyne/status/1209990116757950465)): "Merry Christmas, happy holidays and seasons greetings to all my friends and family across the Galaxy ❤️ May the force be with you! Lots and lots of love, from Allie Samta ❤️ #theriseofskywalker #starwars" ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20200105040512/https://twitter.com/samkkalleyne/status/1209990116757950465)) 196. [↑](#cite_ref-Zibsara_196-0) [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) [CONVENTION REVIEW: COVCON JUNIOR 2022](https://starwarsautographnews.com/2022/03/12/convention-review-covcon-junior-2022) by Williams, Gareth on [starwarsautographnews.com](https://starwarsautographnews.com) ([March 12](/wiki/March_12 "March 12"), [2022](/wiki/2022 "2022")): "A late addition the line-up was Elizabeth Ansari who played x-wing pilot Elna Zibsara in The Rise of Skywalker. It was Elizabeth's first time attending a convention and she did seem a little shocked by all the attention; but was very friendly and appeared really happy to be signing for fans. I know a lot of people like to collect pilots so hopefully we will see Elizabeth at more conventions in the near future." ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220521123633/https://starwarsautographnews.com/2022/03/12/convention-review-covcon-junior-2022) archived on [May 21](/wiki/May_21 "May 21"), [2022](/wiki/2022 "2022")) 197.
